noteIntro_AOO,Journal Tip,Quest Info,,AOO Introduction - READ THIS!,AOO 介紹 - 務必閱讀！
noteIntro_AOODesc,Journal Tip,Quest Info,,"It is the Age of Oblivion! The Turdlinger Research Facility has been overrun by .....things, terrible things. Humanity's only hope is to destroy the research facility. All of this began at the research facility and that is where it must end. Teh facility can be found under Antipas Castle, but you will not be able to enter without killing all of the overlords! There will be 7 quests that you must complete to be able to enter the facility. You can find details about these quests in your journal. Once you have cleared the facility then you must destroy it! Only then we will be able to finally clear the world of all these abominations that originated from this facility. This will not be easy and you should not attempt this on your own. \n\nYour journal has been filled with tutorials to help you along your way and to prepare you for the final fight!",這是遺忘的時代！Turdlinger 研究設施已被......可怕的事物佔領。人類唯一的希望就是摧毀研究設施。這一切始於研究設施，也必須在那裡結束。該設施位於 Antipas 城堡下方，但您必須先殺死所有領主才能進入！您必須完成 7 個任務才能進入該設施。您可以在日誌中找到有關這些任務的詳細資訊。清除設施後，您必須摧毀它！只有這樣，我們才能最終清除源自該設施的所有這些可憎之物。這並不容易，您不應該獨自嘗試。\n\n您的日誌中已填滿教學內容，以幫助您順利進行並為最終決戰做好準備！

noteResearchFacility_AOOEntry,Journal Tip,Quest Info,,"All of this started at Turdlinger's research facility. Something went wrong, no one knows what went wrong but we sure as hell know that it did! It started about 10 years ago when these strange monsters started to appear. At first they were rare and they they were very docile, but that changed quickly. They soon became more abundant and and much more agressive. Within 5 years they had wiped out 95% of the human and animal population. With such large losses the survivors became desperate to find a way to reverse the loss of life. Many of the remaining Scientists experimented with Resurrection, unfortunately this only made things worse. While resurrection was successful"" it was also flawed. After being resurrected it was found that the positive effects were short lived",所有這些都始於 Turdlinger 的研究設施。出了點問題，沒人知道出了什麼問題，但我們他媽的確定它發生了！大約 10 年前，這些奇怪的怪物開始出現。起初它們很稀有，而且非常溫順，但這很快就改變了。它們很快變得更豐富，而且更具侵略性。在 5 年內，它們已經消滅了 95% 的人類和動物。由於損失如此慘重，倖存者迫切希望找到一種方法來扭轉生命的損失。許多剩下的科學家都嘗試了復活，不幸的是，這只讓事情變得更糟。雖然復活成功了，但也有缺陷。在復活後發現積極的效果是短暫的

noteQuickInfoEntry_title,Journal Tip,Quest Info,,AOO Tutorial - Quick Notes,AOO 教學 - 快速筆記
noteQuickInfoEntry,Journal Tip,Quest Info,,"Zombies are now scaled based on your level, if it is night time, if it is blood moon or depending on the Biome. Get started on AOO Quests as soon as you can. AOO quests are important to be able to progress. Always try to have a 1000 Kill Quest active, you get rewards every 100 kills and a bigger reward aftr 1000. Drop box will auto sort item to nearby containers. The free mailbox dropbox is small and slow, There is a better one that you can craft. You do not need the Vanilla Workbench or Chem Station, they are replaced in function by the Oblivion Bench and the Alchemy table.",現在，殭屍會根據你的等級、是否是夜晚、是否是血月或取決於生物群系而調整。盡快開始 AOO 任務。AOO 任務對於能夠進展很重要。始終嘗試讓 1000 殺戮任務處於活躍狀態，你每殺死 100 個就會獲得獎勵，在殺死 1000 個後會獲得更大的獎勵。掉落箱會自動將物品分類到附近的容器中。免費的信箱掉落箱很小而且很慢，有一個更好的你可以製作。你不需要香草工作台或化學工作站，它們的功能已被遺忘工作台和煉金術台取代。
